## Instruction

As a member of the market analysis team, you are urgently tasked with analyzing the price differences between our core product line and our primary competitor, FutureGadget. We have scraped pricing information from our competitor's website (stored in PDF format), and we have also obtained our corresponding product prices from the internal file, internal_pricing_sheet.xlsx. Finally, please combine and process these two sets of data, calculate the price difference, and store the final comparison results (including product name, our price, competitor's price, and price difference) in BigQuery for management decision-making. Please refer to the workspace file requirements.md for storage format requirements.

```json
**BigQuery Storage Requirements:**
- Dataset: `bigquery_pricing_analysis`
- Table: `analysis`
- Full Path: `bigquery_pricing_analysis.analysis`

**BigQuery Table Structure (Required Columns):**
- `Product Name` (String) - Use the exact product name from our internal CSV file
- `Our Price` (Float) - Our product pricing
- `Competitor Price` (Float) - FutureGadget's pricing for similar products
- `Price Difference` (Float) - Calculated as (Our Price - Competitor Price)

**Data Processing Requirements:**
- Use the **Product Name** field from our internal CSV file as the standard product identifier
- Match competitor products to ours based on product features/categories
- Calculate the price difference and store these four columns accurately in the final BigQuery table.
```

```json
{
	"query": "SELECT \n  COUNT(*) as Total_Products,
	\n  ROUND(AVG(`Our Price`),
	 2) as Avg_Our_Price,
	\n  ROUND(AVG(`Competitor Price`),
	 2) as Avg_Competitor_Price,
	\n  ROUND(AVG(`Price Difference`),
	 2) as Avg_Price_Difference,
	\n  SUM(CASE WHEN `Price Difference` > 0 THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) as Products_We_Price_Higher,
	\n  SUM(CASE WHEN `Price Difference` < 0 THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) as Products_We_Price_Lower,
	\n  ROUND(MIN(`Price Difference`),
	 2) as Max_Disadvantage,
	\n  ROUND(MAX(`Price Difference`),
	 2) as Max_Advantage\nFROM `bigquery_pricing_analysis.analysis`"
}
```

```json
{
	"query": "SELECT \n  `Product Name`,
	\n  `Our Price`,
	\n  `Competitor Price`,
	\n  `Price Difference`,
	\n  CASE \n    WHEN `Price Difference` > 0 THEN 'We are more expensive'\n    WHEN `Price Difference` < 0 THEN 'Competitor is more expensive'\n    ELSE 'Same price'\n  END as Price_Position,
	\n  ROUND(ABS(`Price Difference` / `Competitor Price`) * 100,
	 2) as Percentage_Difference\nFROM `bigquery_pricing_analysis.analysis`\nORDER BY `Price Difference` DESC"
}
```

```text workspace/price_analysis_summary.md
# Price Comparison Analysis: Our Products vs FutureGadget

## Executive Summary

I have successfully analyzed the pricing differences between our core product line and FutureGadget's competing products. The analysis has been stored in BigQuery at `bigquery_pricing_analysis.analysis` as requested.

## Key Findings

### Overall Market Position
- **Total Products Analyzed**: 10
- **Average Our Price**: $393.99
- **Average Competitor Price**: $414.88
- **Average Price Difference**: -$20.89 (We are $20.89 cheaper on average)

### Competitive Position
- **Products We Price Higher**: 5 out of 10 (50%)
- **Products We Price Lower**: 5 out of 10 (50%)
- **Maximum Price Advantage**: $200.99 (DataFlow Analyzer)
- **Maximum Price Disadvantage**: -$300.00 (ProcessOptimizer)

## Product-by-Product Analysis

### Products Where We Have Price Advantage (Lower Prices)
1. **ProcessOptimizer**: We're $300.00 cheaper ($899.99 vs $1,199.99) - 25% advantage
2. **NetworkGuard Pro**: We're $100.00 cheaper ($299.99 vs $399.99) - 25% advantage
3. **SecureVault Plus**: We're $49.96 cheaper ($199.99 vs $249.95) - 20% advantage
4. **CloudSync Enterprise**: We're $40.00 cheaper ($89.99 vs $129.99) - 31% advantage
5. **SmartConnect Hub**: We're $40.00 cheaper ($159.99 vs $199.99) - 20% advantage

### Products Where We Price Higher
1. **DataFlow Analyzer**: We're $200.99 more expensive ($1,599.99 vs $1,399.00) - 14% premium
2. **SmartWidget Pro**: We're $50.04 more expensive ($399.99 vs $349.95) - 14% premium
3. **MobileShield**: We're $30.00 more expensive ($79.99 vs $49.99) - 60% premium
4. **AutoTask Manager**: We're $20.00 more expensive ($119.99 vs $99.99) - 20% premium
5. **DataStream Basic**: We're $20.00 more expensive ($89.99 vs $69.99) - 29% premium

## Product Mapping Details

The following mappings were used based on product categories and features:

| Our Product | FutureGadget Product | Rationale |
|-------------|---------------------|-----------|
| SmartWidget Pro | SmartWidget Professional Edition | Direct product match |
| DataFlow Analyzer | DataFlow Business Analyzer | Both enterprise data processing tools |
| CloudSync Enterprise | CloudSync Business Suite | Both cloud synchronization services |
| SecureVault Plus | SecureVault Premium | Both premium security solutions |
| AutoTask Manager | AutoTask Professional | Both task automation tools |
| NetworkGuard Pro | NetworkGuard Enterprise | Both network security solutions |
| DataStream Basic | DataStream Professional | Both data streaming analytics |
| SmartConnect Hub | SmartConnect Enterprise Hub | Both IoT connectivity solutions |
| ProcessOptimizer | ProcessOptimizer Enterprise | Direct product match |
| MobileShield | MobileShield Advanced | Both mobile security solutions |

## Recommendations

1. **Immediate Action Required**: Review pricing for MobileShield (60% premium) and ProcessOptimizer (25% discount) as these show the largest percentage differences.

2. **Competitive Advantage**: Leverage our lower prices on ProcessOptimizer, NetworkGuard Pro, and CloudSync Enterprise in marketing campaigns.

3. **Price Justification**: For products where we charge premiums (especially MobileShield and DataStream Basic), ensure our value proposition clearly justifies the higher cost.

4. **Market Positioning**: Overall, we maintain competitive pricing with a slight advantage, but specific products need attention.

## Data Storage

All analysis data has been successfully stored in BigQuery:
- **Dataset**: `bigquery_pricing_analysis`
- **Table**: `analysis`
- **Columns**: Product Name, Our Price, Competitor Price, Price Difference
- **Records**: 10 product comparisons

The data is ready for further analysis and dashboard creation for ongoing price monitoring.
```
